We designed the curriculum in collaboration with the experts from React Training to ensure that graduates emerge well-prepared to take advantage of dramatically increasing demand for developers with React skills.&l;/p&g;&q;,&q;faq&q;:&q;#Program Overview\n###Why should I enroll in the React Nanodegree program?\nLearning React can significantly improve you skills and career prospects as a front-end developer, and its one of the best career moves you can make right now. React developer job openings are up 160% year-over-year, and React developers are the highest paid developer category. Udacity has partnered with React Training (who regularly provide instruction to Fortune 500 companies, and are the experts behind React Router) to bring you the perfect learning experienceworld-class React instruction with the leading experts in the field, and the through code reviews, career support, and active community of mentors that you can expect from Udacity.\n \n###What kinds of topics will the program cover?\nAs a student of this program, youll master the core principles and fundamentals of React, develop and refine a sense for applying Redux for state management, and build native mobile applications for iOS and Android using React Native library.\n \n###How are you developing the curriculum, and who are your partners?\nUdacity is developing the React Nanodegree program in collaboration with React Training, whose clients include Airbnb, Netflix, The New York Times, and more. Were thrilled to be making their years of experience teaching React to developers at Fortune 500 companies available to you through this new program.\n \n###What jobs will this program prepare me for?\nGraduates of this program will be valuable additions to any team working in the domain of web development, app development, software development, digital marketing, and e-commerce. Opportunities exist in companies ranging from Fortune 500 companies to startups.\n \nSpecific roles include: Front-End Web Developers, Full Stack Web Developers, and UI/UX Developers. For market salary please visit the estimated salary module on the React Nanodegree home page. You&s;ll find industry insights on React in the Stack Overflow 2017 Developer Survey Results.\n \n###What are the prerequisites for this program?\nStudents should have prior development experience building and deploying front-end applications with HTML, CSS, JavaScript, Git, GitHub, NPM, and experience using the command line interface (bash, terminal) .\n \n###What can I do today to ensure I&s;m ready to succeed in the program?\nIf you want to give your skills a refresh, or start in on some advanced preparation, one or more of the following Udacity programs or courses could be perfect for you!\n\n* [JavaScript Design Patterns](https://www.udacity.com/course/javascript-design-patterns--ud989)\n* [Front End Frameworks](https://www.udacity.com/course/front-end-frameworks--ud894)\n* [Version Control with Git](https://www.udacity.com/course/version-control-with-git--ud123) \n* [GitHub &a; Collaboration](https://www.udacity.com/course/github-collaboration--ud456)\n* [Asynchronous JavaScript Requests](https://www.udacity.com/course/asynchronous-javascript-requests--ud109)\n* [ES6 - JavaScript Improved](https://www.udacity.com/course/es6-javascript-improved--ud356)\n \n \n#Software and Hardware\n###Do I need any special equipment to take this program?\nAll students will need a modern personal computer with a text editor (e.g. vim, Sublime Text, Atom, VSCode) \n \n###What frameworks/languages/technologies will this program teach?\nThe React Nanodegree program offers a core curriculum in the React library.\n \n \n#Tuition / Payment\n###How much does the React Nanodegree program cost?\nThe full program consists of one (1) four-month-long Term at a cost of $499, for a total program cost of $499. \n \n###Is there a free trial period for this program?\nThere is no free trial period for this program, but there is a 7-day refund guarantee in place at the beginning of the Term. To request a refund please contact us here. \n \n###Are graduates of the React Nanodegree program eligible for the 50% tuition refund offer?\nNo. React Nanodegree program graduates are not eligible to receive this tuition refund upon completion of their studies. \n \n###Are there scholarships or financial aid available?\nCurrently available scholarship opportunities will be posted on our scholarships page. \n \n \n#Program Structure\n###How is this Nanodegree program structured?\nThe React Nanodegree program is comprised of one (1) Term of four (4) months. A Term has fixed start and end dates. \n \nTo graduate, students must successfully complete 3 projects, , each of which affords you the opportunity to apply and demonstrate new skills that you learn in the lessons. Each project will be reviewed by an expert project reviewer from the Udacity reviewer network. Your reviewer will give you detailed feedback on your work, and either confirm that youve successfully passed the project, or provide you with details on what youll need to improve in order to pass. If you do not pass a project, you will need to make corrections and then submit again, repeating this however many times are necessary until you successfully pass the project. You cannot successfully complete the term until you pass all projects. \n \n###After I graduate, will I still have access to the curriculum?\nYes! Successful graduates retain curriculum access indefinitely. Please note however, that students who leave the programor who are removed from the programprior to successfully graduating, will cease to have access.\n \n###Do you offer the opportunity for students to pause their studies for this program?\nNo. The fixed-term nature of the React Nanodegree program, and the need for maintaining a consistent and stable student body throughout, doesnt allow for offering the option to pause your studies.\n \n###Is this program self-paced?\nNo. The start and end dates of any given Term are fixed, and you must complete all assigned projects by the end date. However, projects may be submitted at any time during a Term, and individual project deadlines are recommendations, not requirements. So within a Term, there is some opportunity to work at your own pace. This program is perfect for beginners.&q;,&q;syllabus&q;:&q;&l;h2&g;What You Will Build&l;/h2&g;\n\n&l;p&g;As you progress through this Nanodegree you will document what you&a;#39;re learning in a web page that you&a;#39;ll build as you go. By the end you will have a fully-functioning web page and some cool programs that demonstrate what you&a;#39;ve learned, like how to:&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;h3&g;Look Professional&l;/h3&g;\n\n&l;p&g;By using a &a;quot;styling&a;quot; language called CSS, you will be able to quickly and easily change the look and feel of your web page. While learning CSS, you&a;#39;ll also gain experience with one of the most important concepts in computer science: avoiding repetition through something called &l;em&g;abstraction&l;/em&g;. &l;/p&g;\n\n&l;h3&g;Display Videos&l;/h3&g;\n\n&l;p&g;In addition to your own notes about what you&a;#39;re learning, you&a;#39;ll learn to write computer code in a language called Python that will embed your favorite videos (from Udacity or anywhere else) directly onto a web page. While learning  Python, you&a;#39;ll be developing a skill that&a;#39;s required for every programming project regardless of language: using procedural thinking to tell a computer exactly what you want it to do.&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;h3&g;Be User-Friendly&l;/h3&g;\n\n&l;p&g;Even though &l;em&g;you&l;/em&g; will have the skills to modify your web page by changing the code it&a;#39;s made from, the people you show it to may not. You&a;#39;ll add a form that allows visitors to add their own content to your page (if you let them of course). While you&a;#39;re learning what to do with information that someone submits to your web page, you&a;#39;ll also gain a deeper understanding for how the internet works and how computer programmers assemble complex programs by combining pieces of computer code that others have written before them. &l;/p&g;\n\n&l;h2&g;How You Will Learn to Build it&l;/h2&g;\n\n&l;p&g;This Nanodegree consists of a series of 5 stages. In each one, you will learn new broadly-applicable technical skills. After each stage, you will complete a project checkpoint, then submit your work for valuable feedback on your progress.  &l;/p&g;\n\n&l;h3&g;Stage 1: Make Your Web Page&l;/h3&g;\n\n&l;p&g;You will learn the basics of how the internet works and how documents written in a language called HTML form the backbone of the Web. In the &l;strong&g;project checkpoint&l;/strong&g; at the end you&a;#39;ll &l;em&g;write HTML and CSS (another language) to make your web page look professional.&l;/em&g;&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;h3&g;Stage 2: Code Your Own Quiz&l;/h3&g;\n\n&l;p&g;This is where you&a;#39;ll learn how to program. You&a;#39;ll learn a programming language called Python and you&a;#39;ll use it to write instructions that the computer can understand and execute. After this stage you will have incredible power: you will be able to automate almost any repetitive task that can be done on a computer. In the &l;strong&g;project checkpoint&l;/strong&g; you will &l;em&g;write a program in Python to build a fill-in-the blanks type quiz.&l;/em&g;&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;h3&g;Stage 3: Create a Movie Website&l;/h3&g;\n\n&l;p&g;In this stage, you will learn an entirely new approach to programming (and thinking) called Object Oriented Programming and how to use this approach to build impressive programs by simply reusing or modifying computer code that others have already written. In the &l;strong&g;project checkpoint&l;/strong&g; you will create a simple movies webpage with images and trailers.*&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;h3&g;Stage 4: Allow Comments&l;/h3&g;\n\n&l;p&g;Up to this point, you still haven&a;#39;t put your web page online: you&a;#39;ve only seen it on your own computer. In this stage, you will gain a deeper understanding for how the internet works and will write code which tells computers called &a;quot;servers&a;quot; how to display web pages. In the &l;strong&g;project checkpoint&l;/strong&g; you will &l;em&g;put your web page online and build what&a;#39;s called a &a;quot;back end&a;quot; which will allow people anywhere in the world to view and--if you let them--modify your site.&l;/em&g;&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;h3&g;Stage 5: Choose Your Next Steps&l;/h3&g;\n\n&l;p&g;At this point, you will already have a solid understanding of most of the essential concepts and skills that programming requires. This stage will be a rapid sampling of some of the ideas that you haven&a;#39;t seen including:&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;ul&g;\n&l;li&g;&l;strong&g;JavaScript&l;/strong&g;: the language of the web.&l;/li&g;\n&l;li&g;&l;strong&g;APIs&l;/strong&g;: &a;quot;Application Programming Interfaces&a;quot; give programmers a way to easily incorporate data from all over the web into their applications.&l;/li&g;\n&l;li&g;&l;strong&g;Recursion&l;/strong&g;: This may be the most mind-blowing idea in programming.&l;/li&g;\n&l;li&g;&l;strong&g;Parallel Computing&l;/strong&g;: How to use many computers to solve really big problems more efficiently.&l;/li&g;\n&l;li&g;&l;strong&g;How to Solve Big Problems&l;/strong&g;: You run into new challenges when you write large programs (or building substantial web pages). &l;/li&g;\n&l;li&g;&l;strong&g;Responsive Web Design&l;/strong&g;: How to make your web page look good on a computer, tablet, or phone.&l;/li&g;\n&l;/ul&g;\n\n&l;p&g;In the &l;strong&g;project checkpoint&l;/strong&g; you will have the chance to &l;em&g;pursue one of these ideas even deeper by adding new functionality (you get to choose what) to your web page.&l;/em&g;&l;/p&g;&q;,&q;tags&q;:[&q;python&q;,&q;javascript&q;,&q;css&q;,&q;html&q;],&q;teaser_video&q;:{&q;transcodings&q;:{&q;480p_1000kbps_mp4&q;:{},&q;480p_mp4&q;:{},&q;480p_ogg&q;:{},&q;720p_mp4&q;:{}}},&q;title&q;:&q;Intro to Programming Nanodegree&q;,&q;tracks&q;:[&q;All&q;],&q;why_nd_summary&q;:&q;&q;,&q;why_nd_data&q;:&q;&q;}]}</script>
